'''

Return on Capital = EBIT / (Net Working Capital + Net Fixed Assets)
	!!! Because we can't get the net working capital and net fixed assets from the API, we'll use the Total assets instead,
		making this ratio more similar to a ROA (annual net income / total assets), as suggested in the book
	Return on Capital v2 = EBIT / total assets

	EBIT: https://api.iextrading.com/1.0/stock/aapl/financials
		under operatingIncome; it's synonymous

	market cap: https://api.iextrading.com/1.0/stock/aapl/quote
		https://api.iextrading.com/1.0/stock/aapl/quote
			~/quote is more realtime
			note: quote also has pe ratio

	total assets: https://api.iextrading.com/1.0/stock/aapl/financials
		under totalAssets

Earnings Yield = EBIT/Enterprise Value
	EBIT:
		operatingIncome: https://api.iextrading.com/1.0/stock/aapl/financials

	Enterprise value = market cap + net debt
		marketcap: https://api.iextrading.com/1.0/stock/aapl/quote
		net debt = total debt - cash and investments:
			totalDebt: https://api.iextrading.com/1.0/stock/aapl/financials
			currentCash: https://api.iextrading.com/1.0/stock/aapl/financials


note: total debt is short term + long term debt
note: cash and investments is equivalent to cash and cash equivalents on balance sheet


~/financials, stats, quote,


Financials:
    EBIT under operatingIncome; it's synonymous
    totalAssets
    totalDebt
    currentCash

Stats:
    nothing needed from here for MVP

Quote:
    marketCap
    ## pe ratio (maybe not)
